					<header class="entry-header">
						
						<h1 class="entry-title">Home</h1>
					</header><!-- .entry-header -->

					<div class="entry-content">
						<div class="post">This is the home page of the Princeton S* Network Systems (SNS) group within Princeton&#8217;s <a title="Computer Science Department" href="http://www.cs.princeton.edu/">Computer Science Department</a>. The undefined S* &#8212; Scalable, Secure, Self-Organizing, Self-Managing, Service-centric, Storage-based &#8212; characterizes the broad scope of our research.</div>
<h3>Projects</h3>
<div class="post">
<table style="weight: 100%;" border="0">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<ul>
<li><a title="Scalable Causal Consistency for Wide-Area Storage" href="http://sns.cs.princeton.edu/projects/cops/">Consistency in Geo-replicated Storage</a></li>
<li><a title="Multi-Tenant Resource Sharing with PISCES" href="http://sns.cs.princeton.edu/projects/pisces/">Cloud Resource Sharing</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<ul>
<li><a title="Untrusted Cloud Storage" href="http://sns.cs.princeton.edu/project/untrusted-cloud/">Services on Untrusted Clouds</a></li>
<li><a title="Passe" href="http://sns.cs.princeton.edu/projects/passe/">Protecting Vulnerable Cloud Applications</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<ul>
<li><a title="JetStream" 
Num bytes read  1448
href="http://sns.cs.princeton.edu/projects/jetstream-and-wide-area-analytics/">Wide-Area Data Analytics (JetStream)</a></li>

</ul>

    <section id="block-system-main" class="block block-system clearfix">
